{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classFoam_1_1GaussField}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classFoam_1_1GaussField}{class}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceFoam_aa8f35761c87b12a7a59a176d2d6c6682}{Foam\+::dg\+Face\+Position}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Face-\/position identifiers for a reference hexahedron. 

Identifies the position of a face on the reference hexahedral element using counter-\/clockwise vertex ordering when viewed from outside the element. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
